At each subsequent visit, cookies are re-sent from the user’s device to the site.<br style=""><br style=""></p><p style="">Cookies allow information about visits to the website to be stored and are very useful as they facilitate the correct functioning of the website, making it more efficient. Without cookies, the website would have no way of “remembering” certain information, such as the contents of the shopping cart. <br style="">The law states that we can only store cookies on your device that are strictly necessary for the operation of this website. For all other types of cookies, we need your consent.<br style=""><br style="">It should be noted that the functionality of a cookie can also be achieved through other <strong style="">similar technologies</strong>, including the use of certain features that allow the owner of the website to identify devices and subsequently analyse visits to the website. This information applies to any technology that stores or accesses information on your device. Technologies that fall into this category include, for example, HTML5 local storage, Local Shared Objects (also called flash cookies) and fingerprinting technologies. From now on, when we talk about cookies, this definition will also include other similar technologies.<br style=""><br style=""><strong style="">What is the purpose of the cookies used by this website?</strong> <br style=""><br style="">This site uses different types of cookies. Some cookies are installed directly from the website (<strong style="">first-party cookies</strong>), while others are installed by third parties, whose services appear on our pages (<strong style="">third-party cookies</strong>).<br style=""><br style=""></p><p style=""><strong style="">Strictly necessary cookies</strong> allow the website to function properly and make it easy for you to use the content and services provided: for example, they allow you to browse the website while keeping the contents of your shopping cart updated or preventing the brief introduction banner from appearing on subsequent visits to the website because your consent has already been recorded. Strictly necessary cookies cannot be disabled, and your prior consent is not required for their installation. The information collected through technical cookies is necessary to allow you to navigate the website correctly.<br style=""><br style=""><strong style="">Analytics cookies</strong> are similar to technical cookies if used directly by the site manager to collect aggregate data on the number of users and how they visit the website. These cookies allow data controllers and/or web site managers to understand how users interact with the site content for optimization purposes. These cookies are not necessary to allow the website to function properly, therefore your consent is required before they are installed.<br style=""><br style=""><strong style="">Advertising and targeting cookies</strong> are used to track navigation and analyse your behaviour on the website in order to personalize advertisements that may be of interest to you. These cookies are not necessary to allow the website to function properly, therefore your consent is required before they are installed.<br style=""><br style="">A complete list of cookies used on this website is available at the bottom of this Cookie Policy.<br style=""><br style=""><strong style="">How can I manage my cookie preferences?</strong> <br style=""><br style="">You can change or withdraw your consent from the Cookie Policy on our website at any time through the appropriate link. The cookie policy can always be reached via a link inserted in the footer of the website.<br style=""><br style="">Please state your consent ID and date when you contact us regarding your consent.<br style=""><br style="">In addition to the above, you can also change your cookie settings through your browser, deleting all or some cookies or limiting the transmission of these same to certain sites. We have listed the instructions for changing the cookie settings in the most common browsers below: &nbsp; </p><ul style=""><li style=""><a href="https://support.google.com/chrome/answer/95647?co=GENIE.Platform=Desktop&amp;hl=it" style="">Google Chrome</a></li><li style=""><a href="https://support.mozilla.org/it/kb/Gestione dei cookie" style="">Mozilla Firefox</a></li><li style=""><a href="https://support.microsoft.com/it-it/help/4468242/microsoft-edge-browsing-data-and-privacy" style="">Microsoft Edge</a></li><li style=""><a href="https://support.apple.com/it-it/guide/safari/sfri11471/mac" style="">Safari</a></li></ul><p style="">&nbsp;</p><p style="">Disabling cookies or deleting them could compromise the optimal use of certain areas of the website or prevent some features from working correctly, in addition to affecting the operation of third-party services.<br style=""><br style=""><strong style="">Communication and dissemination of data</strong> <br style=""><br style="">Data collected using cookies may be processed by employees and collaborators of the company, expressly authorized for such processing and who have received adequate training for such purposes. You also have the right to withdraw your consent for unnecessary cookies without affecting the correct functioning and functionality of the website.
